    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb. 
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox 
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}} 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}} 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex } 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox} 
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert 
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing. 
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line. 
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line. 
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote. 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {% 
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}% 
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}% 
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}% 
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}% 
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}% 
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}% 
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}% 
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}% 
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}% 
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}% 
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}% 
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}% 
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}% 
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}% 
        } 
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized. 
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {% 
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}% 
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active 
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active 
            \lccode`\~`\~ 	
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%
        
        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active 	
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }

\begin{document}
    
    \maketitle
    
    

    
    \hypertarget{iam-writer-recognition}{%
\section{IAM Writer Recognition}\label{iam-writer-recognition}}

    This notebook is pretty much a translation of the
``\href{https://github.com/priya-dwivedi/Deep-Learning/tree/master/handwriting_recognition}{handwriting\_recognition}''
notebook by \href{https://github.com/priya-dwivedi}{Priyanka Dwivedi}. I
have chosen to rewrite it differently here as to make it easier to
follow, for my own better understanding, and for others who wish to
learn from it.

    The goal of the notebook is to use the method explained in the paper
\href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1606.06472}{DeepWriter: A Multi-Stream Deep
CNN for Text-independent Writer Identification} to identify the writer
(author) of a text based on their writing styles. To do so, we'll use
the
\href{http://www.fki.inf.unibe.ch/databases/iam-handwriting-database/download-the-iam-handwriting-database}{IAM
Handwriting Database}. Please make sure the dataset has been correctly
set up before executing the notebook as outlined
\href{https://github.com/diegocasmo/iam_writer_recognition/tree/master/data}{here}.

    \hypertarget{reading-the-dataset}{%
\section{Reading The Dataset}\label{reading-the-dataset}}

    The first step is to create a dictionary which will map each form ID
(sentence) to a writer. This information is available in the
\texttt{forms.txt} file, where each line (except for the first 16 lines,
which are documentation) defines the form ID at index \texttt{0}, and
its writer at index \texttt{1}.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{1}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create a dictionary to store each form ID and its writer}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{os}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{itertools} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{islice}

\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
\PY{n}{forms\PYZus{}file\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{../data/forms.txt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forms\PYZus{}file\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{islice}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{16}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{line\PYZus{}list} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{line\PYZus{}list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{writer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{line\PYZus{}list}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{writer}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Visualize dictionary (as array for simplicity):

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{2}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Number of form\PYZhy{}writer pairs:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Sample form\PYZhy{}writer mappings:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Number of form-writer pairs: 1539
[('a01-000u', '000'), ('a01-000x', '001'), ('a01-003', '002'), ('a01-003u',
'000'), ('a01-003x', '003')]
Sample form-writer mappings: [('a01-000u', '000'), ('a01-000x', '001'),
('a01-003', '002'), ('a01-003u', '000'), ('a01-003x', '003')]
    \end{Verbatim}

    For efficiency reasons, we'll select the 50 most common writers from the
dictionary we have created, and the rest of the notebook will only focus
on them (as opposed to using the 221 authors present in the dataset).

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{3}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Select the 50 most common writer}

\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{collections} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Counter}

\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}writers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}writers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}
\PY{n}{writers\PYZus{}counter} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Counter}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{writer\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{writers\PYZus{}counter}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{most\PYZus{}common}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}writers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}writers}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{writer\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Visualize the writer id of the top 50 writers:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{4}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Top writer IDs:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}writers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}writers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Top writer IDs: ['000', '150', '151', '152', '153']
['000', '150', '151', '152', '153']
    \end{Verbatim}

    From the 50 most common writers we have selected, we'll now need to
select the forms (sentences) they have written:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{5}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{author\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}writer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{author\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}writers}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Visualize the form id of the top 50 writers:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{6}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Number of top forms:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Sample form IDs:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Number of top forms: 452
Sample form IDs: ['a01-000u', 'a01-003u', 'a01-007u', 'a01-011u', 'a01-014u']
['a01-000u', 'a01-003u', 'a01-007u', 'a01-011u', 'a01-014u']
    \end{Verbatim}

    Create a temp directory which contains only the sentences of the forms
selected above:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{7}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{os}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{glob}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{shutil}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create temp directory to save writers\PYZsq{} forms in (assumes files have already been copied if the directory exists)}
\PY{n}{temp\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{../data/temp\PYZus{}sentences}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exists}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{temp\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{makedirs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{temp\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Debugging Line 4: Check if \PYZsq{}top\PYZus{}forms\PYZsq{} is correctly set}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Top Forms: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{original\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{..}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{data}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{sentences}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{*}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{*}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{*.png}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Debugging Line 5: Verify the Paths}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Files found:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{glob}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{glob}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{original\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{file\PYZus{}path} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{glob}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{glob}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{original\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{image\PYZus{}name} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{file\PYZus{}path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sep}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Use os.path.sep for cross\PYZhy{}platform compatibility}
    \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{image\PYZus{}name}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{image\PYZus{}name}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{form\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}forms}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Debugging Line 6: Check if Files are Copied}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Copying file }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{file\PYZus{}path}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ to }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{temp\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{/}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{image\PYZus{}name}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{shutil}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{file\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{temp\PYZus{}sentences\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{image\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Failed to copy }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{file\PYZus{}path}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{. Error: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{e}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Define a couple of constants that will be used throughout the model:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{13}{\boxspacing}

\PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}LABELS} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}
\PY{n}{BATCH\PYZus{}SIZE} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{16}
\end{Verbatim}

    As suggested in the paper, the input to the model are not unique
sentences but rather random patches cropped from each sentence. The
\texttt{get\_augmented\_sample} method is in charge of doing so by
resizing each sentence's height to \texttt{113} pixels, and its width
such that original aspect ratio is maintained. Finally, from the resized
image, patches of \texttt{113x113} are randomly cropped.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{14}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{utils} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{shuffle}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{PIL} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Image}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{random}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{get\PYZus{}augmented\PYZus{}sample}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sample}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sample\PYZus{}ratio}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get current image details}
    \PY{n}{img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Image}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sample}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{img\PYZus{}width} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{img\PYZus{}height} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute resize dimensions such that aspect ratio is maintained}
    \PY{n}{height\PYZus{}fac} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{img\PYZus{}height}
    \PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{img\PYZus{}width} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{height\PYZus{}fac}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Resize image }
    \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{resize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Image}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ANTIALIAS}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img\PYZus{}width} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img\PYZus{}height} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Generate a random number of crops of size 113x113 from the resized image}
    \PY{n}{x\PYZus{}coord} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img\PYZus{}width} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}crops} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x\PYZus{}coord}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{sample\PYZus{}ratio}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}x\PYZus{}coord} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sample}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x\PYZus{}coord}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}crops}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create augmented images (cropped forms) and map them to a label (writer)}
    \PY{n}{images} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}x\PYZus{}coord}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{img\PYZus{}crop} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{new\PYZus{}img}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{crop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Transform image to an array of numbers}
        \PY{n}{images}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asarray}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{img\PYZus{}crop}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{images}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    The model uses a generator in order to be able to call
\texttt{get\_augmented\_sample} when training the model:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{20}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{operator}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{functools} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{reduce}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{utils} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}categorical}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{samples}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sample\PYZus{}ratio}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{while} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:} 
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{offset} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{samples}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}samples} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{samples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{offset}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{offset} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{offset}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{offset} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
            
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Augment each sample in batch}
            \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}samples} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{sample} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
                \PY{n}{label} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
                \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{get\PYZus{}augmented\PYZus{}sample}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sample}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sample\PYZus{}ratio}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}samples}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Flatten out samples and labels}
            \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}samples} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reduce}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{operator}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reduce}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{operator}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}
            
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Reshape input format}
            \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}samples}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Transform input to float and normalize}
            \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{float32}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{255}

            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Encode y}
            \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{augmented\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}categorical}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}LABELS}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{k}{yield} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Create training, validation, and test generators:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{21}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}generator} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{generate\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{BATCH\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

\PY{n}{gpus} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tf}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{config}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{experimental}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{list\PYZus{}physical\PYZus{}devices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{GPU}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{gpus}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{gpu} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{gpus}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{tf}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{config}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{experimental}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}memory\PYZus{}growth}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{gpu}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{RuntimeError} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{23}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{resize\PYZus{}image}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{img}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{tf}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{image}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{resize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    The model used is exactly the same as the one in the
``\href{https://github.com/priya-dwivedi/Deep-Learning/tree/master/handwriting_recognition}{handwriting\_recognition}''
notebook by \href{https://github.com/priya-dwivedi}{Priyanka Dwivedi}:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{24}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{models} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Sequential}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{layers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Dropout}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Flatten}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Lambda}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Activation}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{layers}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{convolutional} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Convolution2D}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ZeroPadding2D}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{MaxPooling2D}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{optimizers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Adam}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{metrics}

\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define network input shape}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ZeroPadding2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{CROP\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Resize images to allow for easy computation}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Lambda}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{resize\PYZus{}image}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} CNN model \PYZhy{} Building the model suggested in paper}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Convolution2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filters}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{32}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size} \PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strides}\PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{same}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{name}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{conv1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Activation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{MaxPooling2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pool\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strides}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{name}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{pool1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Convolution2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filters}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size} \PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strides}\PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{same}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{name}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{conv2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Activation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{MaxPooling2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pool\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strides}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{name}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{pool2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    Next, the model is trained for 20 epochs and the models obtained after
each epoch are saved to the \texttt{./model\_checkpoints} directory

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    Load a saved model weights and use them to predict labels in the test
set:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{26}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}weights\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./model\PYZus{}checkpoints/model\PYZus{}weights.hdf5}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}weights\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}weights}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}weights\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{scores} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{evaluate\PYZus{}generator}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}generator}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{steps}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{BATCH\PYZus{}SIZE}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Accuracy: }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
